<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Work Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head" style="width:100%">String Quartet in D major
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Alt<span class="mh555">ernative</span><span class="ms555">.</span> Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head">String Quartet No.42&#160;; "Russian Quartet No.6"
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composer
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Haydn,_Joseph" title="Category:Haydn, Joseph">Haydn, Joseph</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Opus/Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">Op./Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td><span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://archive.org/stream/JosephHaydnThematisch-bibliographischesWerkverzeichnis/Hoboken1-3#page/n417/mode/2up">Hob.III:42</a></span>&#160;; Op.33 No.6
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">I-Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">I-Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>IJH 429
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Key
</th>
<td>D major
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>4 movements
<ol><li>Vivace assai (D major)
</li><li>Andante (D minor)
</li><li>Scherzo. Allegro (D major) - (Trio) (G major)
</li><li>Finale. Allegretto (D major)
</li></ol>
</td></tr>
<tr>
